1b1(tog gzungs): gronas byed do/ mdapa 'thor dang pazhin du byang chub sems dpa' ya ba kyad de de bzhin na byang rgyam thoms dab sa tu phyin byed pa/ rab 'byor 'di sa ste dpem na/ 
1b2(tog gzungs): da parnand
1b3(tog gzungs): ba sems dpa na pa / ga'adas yin pa de ba nyid dang / chos kyi dbyings nyid dang
1b4(tog gzungs): tsA ba'i rtse bu phyog sa kun pa byed do/ sa dpa tshig gi don byed do// @sa 'dil dper na/ 'i phyis pa
1b5(tog gzungs): gapas nan pa byed do// po 'byod da de bzhin du byu drun sum ma la gnas byed do// rab 'byor dade banan du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' yin po/ sarabakyi
1b6(tog gzungs): rad 'di lta ste dper na/ sU ba'i skem bu'i myig gi 'dus te rog pa'i skyon kyi 'di lta ste dper na/ spu'i skyes bu'i myig la gnas myed do// rna ba dang / mA dang / lce dang / lus dang
2a1(tog gzungs): dbyangs can la phyag 'tshal lo// de rnams la phyag 'tshal te/ bdud kyi 'khor gyis myi tshugs pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs 'di sbyor bar lasa?
2a2(tog gzungs): bdag gi rigs sngags 'di grub par gyurd cig/ 'di lta ste/ a ba me TA/ a pa med/ am pa re/ sam pa re/ ba raM kun dzA ra tra
2a3(tog gzungs): pu ska ra ba ha dza lu khra ma kha yA i li byi li kI lI myi li ki dai rti ba ra mu tre mu tra su khe swA hA/ 'di skad bdag
2a4(tog gzungs): thos pa'i dus gcig na bcom ldan 'das rgyalapo'i khab kyi grong khyer na 'od ma'i tshal bya ka lan ta ka gnas pa na dge slong stong
2a5(tog gzungs): chang ba'i dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po khams cad kyang dgra bcom pazag bzang ba nyon mongs pa med pa/ dbang du gyur pa/

2b2(tog gzungs): sems kyi dbang thams cad kyi dam pa'i pha rol tu son pas stag dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// byang chub sems dpa' khri'i phyag chu'i sems dpa'i dge 'dun
2b3(tog gzungs): chen po 'di lta ste spun po'i ze 'dzind gzhon nur gyu rad pa dang chu lha'i dri gros gzhon nur gyu rad pa dang / bzang po'i blo gros gzhon
2b4(tog gzungs): nur mu dad pa dang rgyal pa'i blo gros gzhon nur gyu rod pa dang 'od kyi blo gros gzhon nur gyur/ ba dang nam mkha'i blo gros gzhon nur
2b5(tog gzungs): gyurd pa dang klog gi blo gros gzhon nur gyur da pa dang 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur da pa dang thub dka' gzhon nur gyurd pa dang chu lha gzhon nur gyu ra
2b6(tog gzungs): dang dri ma byed pa gzhon nur gyur pa dang / byang chub sems dpo' sems dpa' chen po byams pa dang / de dag las bstsogs pa byang chub sems dpa'

3b1(tog gzungs): lhung bzed thogs nas/ rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen por bsod snyoms kyi phyir zhugs pa dang / kund tu rgyu nye rgyal gyis tshe dang ldan pa tsha wu rje spyod yul du zhwa/ sa na sa rgyal po
3b2(tog gzungs): khab kyi grong khyer chen por bsod snyoms kyi phyir song ba mthong ngo // mthong nas de 'di snyam tu sems te/ ci ltar dge slong 'di'i spyod lam padzes pa de/ bubadag gis ldan
3b3(tog gzungs): tshang dge slong ya bram ze 'am/ sor byer chupa gzhan su yang gang la yang sngon sa su thong na bdag de'i kun du song ste/ tshe dang ldan pa khyod kyi
3b4(tog gzungs): pa gang yin/ gang las rab tu zung keng gi chos la dga' zhes dri'o snyam nas do nas kun tu rgya nye rgyal tshe dang ldan pa ta thul gang na pa der song ste

3b6(tog gzungs): phyogs gcig tu gduganadon tu d+hA nye rgyal gyis tshe dang ldan pa rta thul lo 'di skad smras so// / tshe dang ldan pa khyod kyi stond pa ka / gang las rab tu
4a1(tog gzungs): gang gi chos la dga'/ de nas tshe dang ldan pa rta thul gyis kun tu rgyu nyo rgyal la 'di skad ces smras so// shag kya'i sras po rtul zhugs dka' thub chen po kun gyi dam pa
4a2(tog gzungs): dbang ldan pa// 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho pha rol du phyir de cing krol la de bzhin 'gro ba 'grol mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas shes bya sa da yang kyis sdug bsngal mtsho skyems da ltar 'di na yod// 
4a3(tog gzungs): dri ma myed pa de'i skyabs su nga se re re ni de'i tshes le dka'o// nye rgyal gyis smras pa/ khyod kyi stond pa ji skad sA/ ji skad ston / tshe dang ldan pa rta thul gyis
4a4(tog gzungs): smras pa/ de'i phyir tshe dang ldan pa legs sur rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig dang bshad do// das pa nyes su dzum pa 'byung dang / las dang nyon mongs pa dag ldog rgyu de yang
4a5(tog gzungs): 'dren pas rab tu gsungs/ gang na skye dang rgad rgud pa'i sdug bsngal nges par myi gdas par/ pa rang bya'i mchog de smra ba'i khyu mchog de'i rang gi sa mkhyend te
4a6(tog gzungs): gsungs// de nas kund tu rgyu nye rgyal gyis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di thos nasachos rnams la chos kyi myig rdul byed cing dri ma dang bral ba nyon mongs pa med pa skyes te/ des
4b1(tog gzungs): rgyu nad tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu thob nas/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di skad ces smras so// sangs rgyas kyis ni shi nad tu rnyed dpa' bo te rtse bdud rtsi'i chos bshad pa// 'di ni
4b2(tog gzungs): rtag tu skye ba'i 'bab chu skyems par bden pa khong du chud// de ni 'gro ba rnams kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ba ste// lam 'di dam pa shes rab chos rnams sgom
4b3(tog gzungs): pa myi mnyam byed pa yin// de nas kun tu rgyu nye rgol gyis tshe dang ldan pa rta thul la 'di skad ces smras so// tshe dang ldan pa de bzhin gshegs pa dgra/ 
4b4(tog gzungs): bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de da ltarag la bzhugs tshe dang ldan pa ta thul gyis smrapa tshe dang ldan pa bcom ldan 'das ni rgyal po'i khab

4b6(tog gzungs): grogs po'i mchog dang slob ma'i 'khor la bltas ske/ kyi bcom ldan 'das kyi thang du rab tu 'byung ngo // de nas kra dad tu mu nye rgyal tshe dang ldan pa ta thul gyi rkang pa la mgo' bos phyag
5a1(tog gzungs): btsal nas yan gsum bkor pa byas te/ slar song nas ku na tu rku par nas skyes ga la ba der song pa dang / kun tu chu pang nas skyes kyis kun tu rgyu nye rgyal rgyang ring

9b2(tog gzungs): gi ma'i mying ni me'u 'gal zhes bgyi ste/ bdag de las skyes pas na/ de'i slad du bdag gi mying me'u 'gal gyi bu zhes btags so// podag rab tu byung bar yang pha mas gnang lags so//

10a1(tog gzungs): kyis bka' stsal pa// / khyod los 'gro ba 'di dag don 'gror 'drend cing sdug bsngal rgya mtsho rnyed par byed// ra'i lam ni rgyu dang myi rgyu'i 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal rgya mtsho skyems byed pa
10a2(tog gzungs): 'chal pa 'dzes pa rkyen ring mu tshor smra ba wa skad de yang ci zhig zer / khyod ni bcom zi nang bdud kyi las kyis ra la da yang 'dir ni byed myi nus// de nas bdud sdig can gyis dbang phyug chen po'i
10a3(tog gzungs): gzugs phyi sdod par byas nas/ tshangs pa'i cha byad du bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar 'dug ste 'di skad ces smras so// khyod kyi shes rab kyis ni las dang nyon mongs srid pa'i myu gu
10a4(tog gzungs): rab tu bskul // de'i smon can grub pa ci slad sems cad don 'dir 'di ltar sdug bsngal spro// gtso bo 'gro ba 'diran khyod kyi sdod gu dang skye bo gang na'ang ma mchis te/ 
10a5(tog gzungs): dus 'di lags na skyon dang bral khyed ci'i slad du mya ngan myur byi 'ang// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ ras 'dul gang 'khod sems can tshungs med gang ga'i bye ma snyed/ 
10a6(tog gzungs): ngas mthong de dag nga yi spying rjes tha dad par bya ba yin// 'gro ba rab 'bring ngan par gyur pa thard te mthard thug na// de nas mya ngan 'da' yis blo gros ngan pa ci yis skul// de nas yang
10b1(tog gzungs): bdud sdig can sdug bsngal zhing yid myi bde nas yid lu gcags ste/ de nyid du myi sdang bar gyur da nas rang gi gnas su song ste mya ngan gyi khang par zhugs te 'dug pa dang / de'i snod lnga btud kyi gnas na 'khod
10b2(tog gzungs): pa'i sems can kun phan tshun 'di skad du/ ci'i rgyu sde bdag cag gi rgyal po chen po 'di mya ngan gyi khang par zhugs te 'dug pa su yang myi shes so zhes 'dra'o// de nas bdud sdig can gyi bu mo lnga brgya tsam
10b3(tog gzungs): rab tu dga' bar byed pa'i me tog dang / bdug pa dpe spos dang / 'phreng ba dang / thug pa thogs pa rab tu yid 'ong ba'i gos dang che/ lhab lhub kyis bdag cag
10b4(tog gzungs): brgyand nas/ rab tu yid du 'ong 'dre mes par byed pa'i bu'ibye sil ldan byas te/ rab tu yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs kyis klu len kar byed cing yan lag lnga dang ldan pa'i
10b5(tog gzungs): sil snyan dag byas nas dka' ba'i rtsed mo dang ldan par 'dun sdig can gyi satun du 'khod pa dang / bdud sdig can des lag pa gnyis bsgreng nas bos te/ ska ma byed sgra ma byed ces de
10b6(tog gzungs): skad smras pa dang / sud tsam zhig lha'i bu mo dag cad myi ber bu 'khrod de/ yang klu rab tu blangs shing sil snyan byas pa dang / bdud sdig can gyis lag pa gnyis g.yabs te bos so// lhar
11a1(tog gzungs): bu mo de dag gis dka' ba dang ldan pa'i glu dang grwar dang sil snyan lan bdun gyi bar du byas pa dang / yang de bzhin du bdud sdig can de lag pa bsgreng nas 'bod cing sgra ma byed sgra ma byed ces zer
11a2(tog gzungs): de skad ces smras pa dang / lha'i bu mo de dag cang myi zer bar 'khod do// de nas lha'i bu mo dbyangs can glog ces bya bas bdud sdig can ka la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud
11a3(tog gzungs): nes 'di skad ces smras so// gtso bo khyod kyis de'adir shi 'phos ltas shig gzigs sam ci// 'on tam ci zhig de ring 'gro ba bzhugs kyis 'khrugs kyurd tam

11b1(tog gzungs): gang gis kyang // de la de ring mya lus bgyid par dum ma gyichis/ bdud kyis sbas pa/ sbyin dang 'dul zhugs bsam pa sod lam snying rje'i zhags pacad// byung po mtshan pabyed pa'i mdzod/

11b3(tog gzungs): par brtson yid kyis/ dben par rgyu zhing nyes pa ma bu na par bya phyir khor zug du/ cho ga bzhin du zhugs nas grong dang grong khyer song ba dang / rags kyi nang dag ni ro'i srer

12a1(tog gzungs): 'dasol mchod pa bya ba'i phyir lho'i ma ma ston dang / ArI me tog dang / bdug pa dang / spos dang / 'breng ba dang / thug pa dang / lhab sgrub dang / srud pa dang /

12b1(tog gzungs): te bdud sngog can kyi g.yog po lnga brgyams kyis 'dun gyi khang pa de das bram po dun pa'i phyir 'di bu'i me tog kau chen ponas smad kyi tshor gyi ma ma// de dag ring por skye thogs par 'dis

13a1(tog gzungs): ldan 'das// bdag cag mthun par bud byed smad pa yongs spangs nas// blo mchog khyod kyi 'phrul gyis drung du mu dad par ni// mchis nas 'di bzhin thub pa'i dbang po'i

13a4(tog gzungs): ces smras so// nyes byas blo gros can khyod snying po myed g.yo' pa'i// dpal rnyed ci phyir bcom ldan 'dal sdang bar sems// dregs pas gos nas skye

13b1(tog gzungs): 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis 'di 'dra ba'i bdud kyi stobs kyi yul drag po dran par byas la/ gang g.yog mo lnga brgya tsam 'di dag bdag nyid bcing pa lngas bcings par mthong bar

13b3(tog gzungs): byi nad kyis brlabs pa'i phyir ro// de nas g.yog mo lnga brgya na pa de dag bdud sdig can gyi drung nas dong pa dang / de nas bdud sdig can rab tu khros te 'di snyam du sems so//

13b5(tog gzungs): 'khrul nas/ dge slong ko'u ta ma myi mthong zhing slar yang bdag gi gnas su 'ong bar nam mkha' 'di dag pas sa rbad rnam par 'bor rlung dang / rlung dag po chen pos kun
13b6(tog gzungs): khyab par bya'o snyab na yang / sangs rgyas kyi byind kyi rlabs kyi stobs kyi sa rlung cung zad kyang langs par byed ma nus so// zan skra'i rtse lo gcig tsam yang bskyod bcus na mang dul ci spos
14a1(tog gzungs): nas yang bdud sdig can rab tu 'khros shing sdug bsngal te/ yid myi bde'i zhing yid la gcags nas/ tu zhing skad chen pos rang gi bu dang tshogs kyi 'khor la bos te/ bdud

14a3(tog gzungs): 'di sgra ldan g.yon can dag 'jam la// khong nas rang bzhin da dug sdong 'dra ba 'dir skyes so// de nas skra des bdud kyi g.yog po dang / bdud kyi bu mo de dag thams cad
14a4(tog gzungs): dang / bdud kyi bu tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa thams cadarings pa'i gzugs kyis myu rang du lhags na/ bdud sdig can gyi 'dun du 'khor ba dang / 'khor de'i nang
14a5(tog gzungs): nas/ bdud kyi bu rgyal ba'i blo gros shes bya ba des thal mo sbya rad te 'di skad ces smras so// ci'i slad thugs khros rab tu 'khrugs shing thugs mi dges/ sreg bsrel de ring ma byung 'di
14a6(tog gzungs): nas khyod ma 'phos// 'di nas khyod lhag dgra ni su yang ma mchis na// khyod ci rmongs par gyur da ta ma ji skad gzhan du dgongs// bdud kyis smras pa/ shag kya'i bu mo dmangs pa la shing gi
14b1(tog gzungs): grib ma 'dug pa ma mthong ngam/ ci byir 'di na khyod kyi mdun na stobs dang ldan pa'i dgra med smras/ stabs gcig ldan pa g.ye can de yis thams cad rnam pa na mar bslus / bdag cag pu

18a1(tog gzungs): 'gyur// me tog gang gis khyod la mngon gtor ba// phyogs kun tu yang de dag gdugs 'gyur te// dus kund bde ba'i 'byung gnas zhing du ni// gang gnyis/

18a3(tog gzungs): me tog sil pa de dag bcom ldan 'das kyi rdzu 'phrul gyi mthus gang ka'i klung gi bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gi bye ma las 'das pa'i nga me tog gi gdugs/ kun tu 'dug par

18a5(tog gzungs): gyi bar sdang la 'dug go// bdud kyi bu mo de dag dang bdud kyi bu tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa de dag gis kyang so so nas/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs myed
18a6(tog gzungs): dpag tu myed pa thams cad na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das bzhugs shing mtshol bzhes te/ chos kyang 'chad pa 'khor gyis yongs su bskor te/ lham me lhan ne lha rjer bzhugs
18b1(tog gzungs): ba'i kar bu'i gtsug gi drang bad kyi steng gi bar sdang la/ me tog gi gdugs de dag 'dug par gyu rad par mthong zhing / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag kyang / khwa dog mtshungs pa
18b2(tog gzungs): rtags mtshungs pa/ gzugs 'dra ba / mtshungs par ldan pa sha stag la/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag seng ge'i khrel dang ni d+hi/ 'khor ba dang la/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing / 
18b3(tog gzungs): yon tan bkod pa nyis pa dad par mthong ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi dbyangs kyi dkyil la gyi gsung brjod pa ni ma zab mo// 'dun
18b4(tog gzungs): 'khor de dag bcom ldan 'das kyi mthus 'di lta bu'icho 'phrul mi mdzinasamachog tu dga' ba dang thos pa skyes te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs
18b5(tog gzungs): 'go bos phyag 'tshal nas/ chos panyand pa'i phyir spyan sngag 'khod do// de nas brgyad kyi bu tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa de dag las khri phrag bcu byir log nas/ bdud kyi gnas su de la bu
18b6(tog gzungs): ngo mtshar/ bdud sdig can la rgya cher bzlas te/ dge slong ko'u ta ma de'i sku'i khung bu gcig kyang bdag cag gis gzhig ma nus na/ gsad pa lta ci gos/ de'i steng du nyi khri de'i skyabs su song
19a1(tog gzungs): ste/ chos mnyand pa'i phyir de'i mdun na 'khod do// de nas btud sdig can rab tu 'khros te sdug bsngal zhing yid myi bde nas yid la gcag te dres 'di skad ces smras so// shag kya'i bu ni ci srid
19a2(tog gzungs): brlag par ma byas pa// de srid bar du ra'i dpal song slar myi 'ong // shag kya'i bu 'di ji ltar de ring bsad snyam ste// bdag cag gzhan la yid myi rtog cing myi smra gdug/ de nas
19a3(tog gzungs): btud sdig can yid myi bde zhing mya ngan gyi khang pa na 'dug ko// / 'dul rin po che tog/ gi gzungs las/ bdud spa bkod pa'i le'u ste dang po'o// 
19a4(tog gzungs): de nas bdud kyi bu mo dang / bdud kyi bu tshogs kyi 'khor sa pa de dag gis bcom ldan 'das/ 
19a5(tog gzungs): la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cog ni 'di lta bu'i zag pa dang / ye shes dang / rdzu 'du3/ snyi mdzo dang / thabs dang / spobs pa 'tshal to/ 
19a6(tog gzungs): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thabs dang ye shes kyi bar du ldan pa ngo mtsha rad to// bcom ldan 'das chos du dang ldanan skyes bu gang reg smin pa grogs po'i lag tu kyi 'chi zhing
19b1(tog gzungs): myu rangad du bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal darigs kyi bu dag tshes bzhi drang ldan na/ 'di la skyes
19b2(tog gzungs): bu gang zag la la sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag du myi 'gro zhing myu rang du bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// bzhi gang zhe na bzhin 'angs dag
19b3(tog gzungs): 'di la rigs kyi bu chos thams cad la mchog tu myi 'dzin da cing / chos gang yang yongs su myi 'dzind myi gtong / khas mye lend nye bar myi lend myi rtog
19b4(tog gzungs): rnam par myi rtog go// 'di lta ste sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyi nad pa la spyod pa na/ sbyin pa'i 'bras bu yang myi gtong myi 'dzind/ khas myi len de/ nye bar myi lend/ myi gnas
19b5(tog gzungs): myi rtog/ rnam par myi tog ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyi nad pa'i bar du spyod pa na/ myi tog pa rnam par myi rtog pa'i bar du'o// bzhin bzangs dag gzhan yang rigs kyi bu de sems can
19b6(tog gzungs): du smra ba ma yin// srog du smra ba ma yin gseral bar smra ba ma yin pa/ gang zag du smra ba ma yin/ sems can gyi khams la yid kyis mchog tu myi 'dzidad pa nas/ myi rtog rnam par
20a1(tog gzungs): myi rtog pa'i bar du'o// bzhin bzangs dag gzhan yang rigs kyi bu de/ gzugs dang / sgra dang / dri dang / ro dang / reg bya la mchog tu myi 'dzind pa nas/ myi rtog
20a2(tog gzungs): rnam par myi rtog pa'i bar du'o// bzhin bzangs dag gzhan yang rigs kyi bu de khams gsum dang / dus gsum dang / phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched rnams kyi rgyu dang
20a3(tog gzungs): rkyend dang / dmyigs pa dang / 'bras bu rnam par smin/ bar 'byung ba dang / gnas dang / skye ba thams cad la mchog tu myi 'dzind pa nas/ myi rtog rnam par
20a4(tog gzungs): myi rtog pa'i bar du'o// de ci'i phyir zhen/ khams cad mkhyend pa'i ye shes ni/ pyod pa'i gnas kyi yul thams cad kyi dang rnabu zur rtog pa dang bral
20a5(tog gzungs): ba ste/ myi dmyigs pa'i tshul gyis spyad par bya'o// bzhin bzang dang chos thams cad dang / thams cad mkhyend pa nyid ni dngo pa myed pa yin te/ sgra myed pa/ mtshan ma med pa
20a6(tog gzungs): yi ga myed pa/ smond pa myed pa/ skye ba myed pa/ 'gag pa myed pa mtshan nyid myed pa/ chags pa myed pa/ dmigs pa myed pa/ bstand du myed pa/ dben pa bdag myed pa
20b1(tog gzungs): mtshan nyid dang bral ba/ skad cig pa/ nye bar zhi ba/ mun pa myed pa/ snang ba myed pa/ gnas myed pa/ yul myed pa dbang po myed pa/ phyogs myed pa/ gnyen de med pa/ bsam/ 
20b2(tog gzungs): du myed pa/ myi 'phrogs pa ser sna myed pa spros pa myed pa/ rdul myed pa rdul dang bral ba/ cha shas myed paci yang byed pa/ byed pa po myed pa/ tshor 'aye byed pa
20b3(tog gzungs): rten da myed pa gzung ba myed pa rnam par rig pa byed ba so sor snang ba myed pa skad cig ma yin pa'i bar du'o// ngas dag kyims cad mkhyend pa
20b4(tog gzungs): nyid na nim mkha' dang mtshungs te stong pa nyid pas dmyigs su byed pa'i tshul dang / myi gnas pa'i tshul dang / mchog tu 'dzidod pyad pa'i tshul dang / kyi rtog
20b5(tog gzungs): rnam par myi rtog pa'i tshul gyis spyad par bya'o// bzhin bzangs dag chos bzhi po de dag dang ldan na/ skyes bu gang zag sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag du myi 'gro zhing myu rad du
20b6(tog gzungs): bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// bzhin bzangs dag gang la la yul thams cad la chags pa'i lus kyi mtshan nyid kyi gnas la rnam par
21a1(tog gzungs): dpyod pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes tshol na/ de gnyis la chags pa yin te/ de gnyis la chags pa'i yid kyi brnag pa ni/ thams cad mkhyen pa
21a2(tog gzungs): nyid su bar byed do// de la gnyis gang zhen// gang srung po dang / khams dang / skye mched rnams la mtshan nyid du rnam par 'apyod pas/ gnas pa dang / mchog tu 'dzind pa de ni gnyis te/ 
21a3(tog gzungs): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid slu ba'o// spyod pa'i gnas dadang / 'bras bu la rtog pa 'di ni gnyis so// skye ba dang srid pa dang / lend pa dang / sems can gyi gnas/ 
21a4(tog gzungs): la rtog pa 'di ni gnyis so// bshad pa dang / rab tu bstand pa dang / gdams pa dang / tshig gi lam dang sgra dang / skad kyi gad na la rtog pa 'di ni gnyis so// 
21a5(tog gzungs): rtag pa dang / chad pa la rnam par lta ba'i shes pa dang / shes bya'i gnas la rtog pa 'di ni gnyis so// sems can dang / sreg dang gso'o ba dang / skyes bu dang / gang zag dang / 
21a6(tog gzungs): byed pa po dang / byed du 'dug pa'i 'du shes kyi gnas la rtog pa 'di ni gnyis so// gang pa rol dang / tshu rol dang / rtog pa dang / si la pa la gnas shing rtog pa 'di ni gcim zon
21b1(tog gzungs): bzhin bzangs dag skyes bu gang zag su la la thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes tshol ba de/ dus gsum du ngang 'dzind pa dang nga yir 'dzind pa dang kun 'byung ba da na lagaka pa dang / 
21b2(tog gzungs): rnam par dpyod pa la gnas shing / kun tu rtog ste/ mchog tu 'dzin na 'di ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la de gnyis so// 'di lta ste dper na/ skyes bu zhig ma dad pa la
21b3(tog gzungs): sa'i ngos la nyug pa dang / skos 'dod pa la me dang / na 'dod pa la rdo dang / me tog 'dod pa la gos dang / spos 'dod pa ro bas pa dang gos 'dod pa la dur
21b4(tog gzungs): khrod dang / thug pa 'dod pa la dam mkha' la nyug pa de bzhin du bzhin bzangs dag gang spyod pa'i gnas la chags shing rnam par spyod pa'i lus gnyis kyi gnas/ 
21b5(tog gzungs): gnyis kyis thams cad mkhyend pa'i ye shes tshol na de'i 'bad pa 'bras bu byed pa yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gzungs kyi blo gro pa zhes bya ba
21b6(tog gzungs): 'khor der 'dus par gyurd nas 'dug pa des/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der logs su thal mo srung ba btud te/ 'di skad ces gsolan to// bcom ldan 'das gang brjod du ma mchis pa
22a1(tog gzungs): de mngon par rdzoms par 'tshang tu byam dus la gsus s+ho bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' spel da pa/ gang brjod du med par shes pa de nyid madrod par rdzog su
22a2(tog gzungs): tshang rgya'o// de'i phyir rigs kyi bu khyod nyid la drim thama'i ltar ba'od pa de bzhin du la nad thob cig gang thams cad mkhyen pa thob par 'gyur ba'i rjes kyi mtshan nyid
22a3(tog gzungs): kyi dngos po gang yod dam gsolade pa/ gal te mchi skyes shes bgyi na ni rtag par 'gyur/ ji ste ma mchis zhes 'byin ni chad par 'gyur ro// shul
22a4(tog gzungs): ma'i lam ni dmyigs su ma mchis te/ de ni mchis pa 'ang ma lags/ ma mchis pa 'ang ma lag so// kang pa chags/ myi skye/ mya 'ag
22a5(tog gzungs): tshad ma mchis grangs ma mchis/ dpe' ma mchis/ snang ba ma mchis pa de la 'tshal po 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par te tshang rgya ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' brog
22a6(tog gzungs): gi blo gros kyis gsol pa bcom ldan 'das gang la yang 'gro ba 'ang ma mchis/ 'ong ba 'ang ma mchis pa de lta bu shes pa la 'jug par mi khas po 'di ni myi
22b1(tog gzungs): mngon du bgyi ba 'ang ma mchis/ zhi ba 'ang ma mchis/ rab tu zhi ba 'ang ma mchis/ dus gsum yang ma mchis/ theg pa gsum yang me mchisasmon ldum dang mnyam pa'i
22b2(tog gzungs): rlom sems kyang ma mchis pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi blo gros kyis gsol pa bcom ldan 'das gang khyams gas
22b3(tog gzungs): yang ma mchis kund tu sbyor ba gsum yang ma mchis rig pa gsum yang ma mchis theg pa gsum yang ma mchis / phung po dang / khams dang
22b4(tog gzungs): skye mched la rtog pa yang ma mchis rnam par rtog payang ma mchis bri ba yang ma mchis/ 'phel ba yang ma mchis la mnyam par yang mya bgyid pa

22b6(tog gzungs): chos dang / kyi slob pa'i chos dang/ nyan thos kyi chos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams la myi rtog rnam par myi rtog ste mnyam par yang myi bgyid pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs
23a1(tog gzungs): 'chang bya ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' sra ba'i blo gros kyis gsol pa gang dben pa'i tshul gyis de bzhin nyid la rnam par dpyod cing / mngon par myi zhed pa 'di ni mngon par
23a2(tog gzungs): rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' phyag na rin pos gsol pa/ gang chos thams cad myi skye ba'i mtshan nyid thob par bgyi ba dang / mngon par rtogs par bgyi ba'i slad

23a4(tog gzungs): par dpyod cing sems nyid sems la 'dug par bgyid de/ sems gnyi ka la sems kyis rnam par dpyad nas myi myigs pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o// 
23a5(tog gzungs): byang chub sems dpa' dgra las rnam par rgyal gyis gsold pa gang chos thams cad la mya chags/ rjes su myi chags/ btang snyoms su myi bgyid/ khong khro bar myi bgyid/ 'dod par

23b1(tog gzungs): chags shing / zab mo la bzod pa'i tshul la 'dug pas ngang 'dzind pa dang / nga yid 'dzin pa la myi tog pa 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o// blo 'od gzhon nur gyur na bas

23b4(tog gzungs): pa dang / 'phel ba dang / 'bring ba thams cad kyi 'byung 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'phang rgya ba'o// bya 'aM sems de pa'i rtsos pas g.yel dpa/ gang gnas
23b5(tog gzungs): la gnas pa na ga khams gsum pa la gnas pa'i tshangs pa la myi dmyigs mnyam par myi bgyid pa 'di ni/ mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' blo gros kyi
23b6(tog gzungs): bzad pas gsol dpa gang 'khor gsum yongs su dag pas pha rol tu phyind pa rnams la myi dmyigs pa'i tshul gyis rab tu goms par bgyid cing myi chags kyi skyo ba 'di ni mngon par rdzogs
24a1(tog gzungs): par 'chang rgya ba'o// 'jab dpal gzhon nur gyur da pas gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gang chos thams cad la myi chags kyi skyo zhing / chos zab mo'i tshul yang rab tu 'tshal da te/ 
24a2(tog gzungs): gang rab tu 'tshal ba de yang myi le nad mi 'dod / sdud par myi bgyid 'bral bar myi bgyid cing / chos gang la yang bathogs pa 'am/ 'bri ba 'am/ rig pa 'am/ rnam par grol ba 'am/ 
24a3(tog gzungs): 'jig pa 'am/ 'bri ba 'am/ 'phel ba yang myi bsgre da da la/ dngos po dag la rnam par myi rtog pas/ kun nas nyon mongs par myi 'gyur ba 'di ni mngon par rdzogs par 'tsha
24a4(tog gzungs): rgya ba ste/ tshul gcig po 'dis thams cad mkhyenapa'i ye shes mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ltad mo can gyis smras pa/ 'ja
24a5(tog gzungs): dpal de bzhin nyid la 'jug pa'i tshul 'di ltar zab mo stong pa nyid sgom pa'i tshul gcig gis thams cad mkhyend pa'i ye shes mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya na/ kund tu spyo pa dang
24a6(tog gzungs): rab tu spyor par ci skos/ 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ lta ba myi bzad pa dang bral zhing yang dag pa'i lte bar sgro 'dogs pa yang myed pa dang / g.yo'i myed cing drang por sgro 'dogs pa
24b1(tog gzungs): yang myed pa dang / sdig pa dang bral zhing bla ma la ri mor bya bar sgra 'dogs pa yang myed pa dang / bka' blo bde bar sgro 'dogs pa yang myed pa dang / yang dag pa'i mtsho bar sgro 'dogs pa yang

25a1(tog gzungs): myed pa dang / rdul dang mun pa'i phung po thams cad spong bar sgro 'dogs pa yang myed pa dang / bsngo ba'i 'bras bu rnam par smind pa thams cad spong bar sgro 'dogs pa yang myed pa
25a2(tog gzungs): 'di dag ni rigs kyi bu thams cad mkhyend pa'i ye shes kyi sbyor ba nyi shu ste/ yi ge dang skad dang / skra dang smra ba dang / brjod pa'i tshig rab tu dbye ba thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid shes pa la 'dug pas
25a3(tog gzungs): thams cad mkhyend pa'i ye shes kyi sbyor ba'o// gzhan mu stegs can gyi tshig gi de bzhin nyid la 'dug pa dang / spyod pa thams cad kyi de bzhin nyide la 'jug pa dang / bsod

25a5(tog gzungs): la 'jug pa dang / rnam par tha rad pa gsum dang gnas dang / rgyu dang / las dang / chos thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid la 'jug pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' tham
25a6(tog gzungs): shes nas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi spyor pa khang du chud par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa' ltad mo can gyis smras pa/ 'jam dpel de bzhin te/ nam chos 'bri ba rje

25b2(tog gzungs): kang rab tu spong ba dang / gang skom pa dang / gang kun shes par 'gyur ba'i chos de dag thams cad brjod du myed pa'i tshul gyis de bzhin nyid la 'dujug ste/ des thams cad mkhyend pa'i ye shes
25b3(tog gzungs): khong du chud par 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa legs so legs so// rigs kyi bu tshul gcig kis thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'thob pa de khyod kyis
25b4(tog gzungs): legs par smras so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ thams cadal chags pa myed pa'i dngos po yin pas chos thams cad ni sgro btags pa myed pa dang / ma skyes pa dang
25b5(tog gzungs): myi 'jig pa'i mtha' can dang / ma rig pa dang / mya ngan las 'odas pa skye ba ga pa'i mtha' can dang / chos thams cad ni brjod du myed pa'i mtha' can dang / sems can thams cad kyang
25b6(tog gzungs): de lta bu yin pa dang chos thams cad ni rdzas myed pa'i mtha' can dag dus gsum dang / khams gsum dang / phung po thams cad ni ji yang myed pa'i mtha' can dang / 'du byed gsum ni stong/ 
26a1(tog gzungs): na pa'i ba dang / rjod pa byed pa'i dod dang / rtsom pas khyod kyi sa bams pa dang ldan pa'i bya chul sems dpa' sems dpa tshan du sems cad mabyen pa'i
26a2(tog gzungs): no// sa das dadashes pa la lang smra 'di ga pa'i/ kyi ma/ 
26a3(tog gzungs): ba'i chos la bzod pa thob ste/ lus rags pa spangs nas/ yid kyi sus rnyed do// zhan nyi brgyad spang gson kyi skye ba'i chos la 'dzad pa thob par
26a4(tog gzungs): gyu rad to// lha dang myi dkrigs phrag dgu bcu sa gnyis kyis ni byang chub sems dpa'i bzod pa dang / ting nge 'dzind dang / gzungs sna tshogs thob par gyur to// degs byang chub
26a5(tog gzungs): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mye skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob pa nyi khri bo de dag gis bcom ldan 'das la lha'i me tog gis gtong/ rab tu gtod nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs
